[1/17/25, 5:20:50â€¯PM] Skip Tan: Noted Sir.

This was due to partial usage of syrup for C-graining which lessen syrup for CVP-A sugar production.
This happened due to no c-light molasses (used for syrup alternative) caused by stoppage of double purging.
During yesterday's 3rd shift, I allowed SIC to stop double purging temporarily and utilize double purging CCBs for C-massecuite purging. This was due to increasing level of C-massecuite level caused by 5 out of 7 CCBs running. The 2 CCBs are the large capacity CCBs, #8 (13tph) and #10 (14tph), which cannot be completely compensated by the remaining CCBs.

I decided this way to avoid molasses congestion at pan boiling and ultimately mill stoppage.

[2/22/25, 10:42:06â€¯AM] ~â€¯Murugesan: Good morning 
A and B footing preparation procedure
1. Check the magma quantity is sufficient for footing 
2. Pull magma up to 1st sight glass level 
3. Close the cutover valve and wait for boiling pickup  
4. Increase the magma brix slightly more than the boiling brix 
5. Open the condensate water clean the lower level fine grains 
6. Make sure uniform and sufficient crystal 
7. Wait for boiling brix
8. Start feed with normal boiling brix
9. Feed continuously with normal boiling brix (No batch feeding)
10. No too light and too heavy boiling
